<analysis>**original_problem_statement:**
The user provided a list of 12 security fix recommendations from a tool called Codex and requested an assessment and implementation of the critical ones. Subsequently, the user reported a series of bugs: a role-based deletion error, a choppy file upload experience, a non-functional deployed application due to a  misconfiguration, and incorrect item grouping for  users.

Finally, the user requested a major feature to implement a staged partial update for physical stock, including a preview/approval modal and a robust upload queue. This was followed by two rounds of corrections and patches to make the feature date-safe, prevent global data wipes, and harden the data matching logic to be stamp-aware and handle ambiguity.

**PRODUCT REQUIREMENTS:**
1.  Analyze and fix critical security vulnerabilities from the Codex report.
2.  Fix a bug preventing  users from deleting their own entries.
3.  Improve the reliability of the file upload UI.
4.  Fix a deployment issue caused by  excluding  files.
5.  Correct the item display for polythene executives to show individual items instead of grouped items.
6.  Implement a new physical stock upload workflow that supports staged partial updates with a preview/approval modal.
7.  Refactor the frontend upload logic into a serialized queue to handle uploads reliably.
8.  Make all physical stock operations (full snapshot replacement, partial updates) strictly date-scoped to prevent data corruption across different dates.
9.  Harden the physical stock matching logic to use stamps when available and to detect and report ambiguity when a stamp is missing for duplicate item names on the same date.

**User's preferred language**: English

**what currently exists?**
The application's security has been further hardened by implementing several high-priority Codex recommendations, including adding admin role checks to bulk write endpoints and fixing an upload session ownership vulnerability. A series of user-reported bugs related to permissions, UI reliability, deployment, and data display have been resolved.

A sophisticated, date-scoped physical stock management feature now exists. It supports two distinct workflows:
1.  **Full Snapshot Replacement**: A date-safe mechanism to replace the entire physical stock for a specific day without affecting data from other dates.
2.  **Partial Update Preview/Apply**: A workflow to upload a partial list of items, preview the changes (gross/net weight deltas), and apply them individually or all at once for a specific date.

The frontend features a robust, serialized upload queue, ensuring files are processed one at a time reliably. The backend matching logic for physical stock is now stamp-aware and detects ambiguity, preventing incorrect data updates.

**Last working item**:
-   **Last item agent was working**: Patching the physical stock feature to enhance safety and correctness. This involved four main fixes:
    1.  Modifying the frontend  to ensure  files are never sent through the chunked upload path.
    2.  Refactoring the backend  to make both direct () and chunked uploads for physical stock date-safe, eliminating global  calls by extracting a shared helper function ().
    3.  Hardening the preview endpoint's matching logic to be stamp-aware and to return an  status for items that have duplicate names on the same date when no stamp is provided in the upload file.
    4.  Updating the frontend preview modal to display warnings for these ambiguous items.
-   **Status**: COMPLETED

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:

                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/master-items'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/master-items': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/master-items?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/upload/init'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/upload/init': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/upload/init?

        batch_id = f"TEST_weight_conv_purch_{uuid.uuid4()}"
        headers = ["Item Name", "Type", "Party Name", "Net.Wt.", "Fine", "Gr.Wt.", "Date"]
        # Net.Wt. = 1.5 KG = 1500 grams
        # Fine = 1.38 KG = 1380 grams
        # Gr.Wt. = 1.6 KG = 1600 grams
        rows = [
            ["Purchase Weight Test", "P", "Supplier", "1.5", "1.38", "1.6", "2024-07-02"]
        ]
    
        response = session.post(f"{API_URL}/upload/client-batch", json={
            "file_type": "historical_purchase",
            "batch_id": batch_id,
            "year": "2024",
            "headers": headers,
            "rows": rows,
            "is_final": True
        }, timeout=30)

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/health', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/health': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/health?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/health', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/health': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/health?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/auth/login': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/auth/login?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/analytics/sales-summary'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/analytics/sales-summary': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/analytics/sales-summary?

params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/health', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/health': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///health?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/master-items'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/master-items': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/master-items?

self = <PreparedRequest [GET]>, url = '/api/analytics/supplier-profit'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/analytics/supplier-profit': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/analytics/supplier-profit?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/analytics/smart-insights'
params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"
            )
E           requests.exceptions.MissingSchema: Invalid URL '/api/analytics/smart-insights': No scheme supplied. Perhaps you meant https:///api/analytics/smart-insights?

self = <PreparedRequest [POST]>, url = '/api/auth/login', params = OrderedDict()

    def prepare_url(self, url, params):
        """Prepares the given HTTP URL."""
        #: Accept objects that have string representations.
        #: We're unable to blindly call unicode/str functions
        #: as this will include the bytestring indicator (b'')
        #: on python 3.x.
        #: https://github.com/psf/requests/pull/2238
        if isinstance(url, bytes):
            url = url.decode("utf8")
        else:
            url = str(url)
    
        # Remove leading whitespaces from url
        url = url.lstrip()
    
        # Don't do any URL preparation for non-HTTP schemes like `mailto`,
        # `data` etc to work around exceptions from `url_parse`, which
        # handles RFC 3986 only.
        if ":" in url and not url.lower().startswith("http"):
            self.url = url
            return
    
        # Support for unicode domain names and paths.
        try:
            scheme, auth, host, port, path, query, fragment = parse_url(url)
        except LocationParseError as e:
            raise InvalidURL(*e.args)
    
        if not scheme:
>           raise MissingSchema(
                f"Invalid URL {url!r}: No scheme supplied. "
                f"Perhaps you meant https://{url}?"

**Critical Info for New Agent**
1.  **Physical Stock Has Two Workflows**: Be aware of the two distinct physical stock operations: 1) Full, date-scoped snapshot replacement (), and 2) Partial, date-scoped preview-and-apply updates (, ). Do not confuse them.
2.  **All Physical Stock Ops are Date-Scoped**: The most critical change in this session was making all physical stock operations safe by scoping them to a . Global operations that wipe the entire collection have been eliminated.
3.  **Frontend Uploads are Queued**: The  now processes all uploads (including the legacy ones) through a serialized queue, one at a time. The  upload type is now always routed to the direct preview flow, never chunked.
4.  ** is Fragile**: Continue to exercise extreme caution when modifying . The next major task should ideally be proposing a plan to refactor it.
5.  **New Tests are the Source of Truth**: The most recent and relevant tests are in  and . Older test files have known, pre-existing issues.
